[38;5;130mINSERT[m [35mINTO[m RankTopThree(Rank, Car_Make,Car_ID,Total_Score)[38;5;130mSELECT[m MIN(Rank), Car_Make,Car_ID,Total_Score [35mFRR[21;1HOM[m RankWithTotal [35mGROUP[m [35mBY[m Car_Make [35mORDER[m [35mBY[m Rank;
